[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresence but not necessarily causing the hang.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The hang persists long enough that libFuzzer’s default timeout threshold [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m seconds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is exceeded.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • PDFExtractTextFuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry point, input handling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • PDFTextStripper methods, especially `processPages`, `writeText`, and `getText`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • PDPageTree traversal logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`iterator`, `enqueueKids`, `getKids`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • COSDictionary methods, notably `getCOSArray` and associated data flow [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallbacks.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Native tracing integration [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm it does [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot introduce unbounded waits.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic investigation should map how the fuzzer-generated PDF input exercises [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDFBox’s page tree and dictionary processing, and whether certain structures or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallback interactions can cause unbounded traversal or blocking.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
